10,"New Release v0.7 + new website!","new-release-v07-new-website","","<p><img style="float: right;" alt="inv-small" src="images/stories/inv-small.png" height="150" width="150" /></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">Hi guys. I would like to welcome you to our new website!</span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">So this is our first big release since a while implementing the  inventory system together with a few more features.</span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p /><span style="font-size: 12pt;" /> \r
","</span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">Here is a complete list of the  new features:</span></p>\r
<p><br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Persistent storage system on server side. Players will now need  to create a game account where all their data will be saved for each  world they will visit player position in world,inventory,etc.)</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - New game website:  you can find our new game website at this  address:  <a href="../%7Elbanetweb" target="_blank">sd-1287.dedibox.fr/~lbanetweb</a>. The site is still under  construction and our great designer and webmaster leoboe is still  working on it. However,you can already register a game account there to  be able to play the game.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Inventory system:  the player will get an independent inventory  for each world. A new GUI is then available in game were the player can  visualize his current inventory content.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Container system: the player can open different containers in the  world. Then he will be able to take objects from the containers or add  objects from his own inventory into the containers.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Shortcut bar: a new in game shortcut bar has appeared. You can  drag and drop items from your inventory into it.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - New whisper functionality: players can now whisper to each other.  To do so you can either tape ""/w playername message"" in your chatbox or  choose whisper in the channel menu.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Friend functionality: you can now add people to your friend list  in the community window.  You will then be able to easily see which of  your friends are online. You can also directly whisper to them by right  clicking on their name in the community window.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Faster map loading: some optimizations have been made server-side  to decrease the loading time of maps.</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Added a map created by Polaris in tippet island</span><br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> - Few bugs fixes.</span><br /> <br /> <br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> Finally you will notice that you cannot anymore ride the horse, dino-fly or use the protopack in the lbaexpanded world. Indeed,the  corresponding items have been hidden all over the world. It is your task  to find them out   ;)</span></p>\r

9,"Game installation","game-installation","","<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>Before installing the game please make sure that you have the .NET platform 3.5 installed on your machine. If not you can download it there: </strong></span>[URL="http://www.microsoft.com/downloads/details.aspx?FamilyId=333325FD-AE52-4E35-B531-508D977D32A6&amp;displaylang=en"]here[/URL]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>In order to play the game you will also need to install Nvidia PhysX on your machine. If you do no have it already you can download it </strong></span>[URL="http://www.nvidia.com/object/physx-9.10.0223-driver.html"]here[/URL]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">There is two ways to install the game on your machine:</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Using the installers recommanded windows XP):</strong></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">[LIST] [*]Download and install the game installer: [URL]http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LbanetSetup.msi[/URL] [*]Download and install the images files installer: [URL]http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LbanetImageSetup.msi[/URL] [*]Start the game from startup menu or desktop icon <img src="plugins/editors/jce/tiny_mce/plugins/emotions/img/smiley-cool.gif" alt="Cool" title="Cool" border="0" />[/LIST]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Manual installation from archive files recommanded windows vista and 7):</strong></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">[LIST=1] [*]Download and unpack the game archive: [URL]http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LBANet_v0.7.rar[/URL] [*]Run LBANet.exe <img src="plugins/editors/jce/tiny_mce/plugins/emotions/img/smiley-cool.gif" alt="Cool" title="Cool" border="0" />[/LIST]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Game requirements:</strong></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">[LIST] [*]The game has been tested on the following platforms: Windows XP,Windows Vista 32bit and 64bit) and Windows 7 32bit and 64bit). [*]It was also tested and could run under Mac OSX using Parallels [*]There is no supported linux version for now,but it is planned [*]The game will not run under windows 2000 because IPV6 is not supported there. [*]There is no real minimum requirements,however your graphic card needs to have drivers supporting OpenGL for the game to run correctly. Also your graphic card need to support texture size of at least 2048x2048 [/LIST]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>Windows 7 and Vista users: the game and game the patcher may need administrator rights to run properly. In order to do it,go in the game directory. Right click on Lbanet.exe. Click on Property in the context menu. Go to the compatibility tab. Check the box "run as administrator". Click the OK button.</strong></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong><br /></strong></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">If you run into trouble installing or playing the game,please post your problem [URL="http://forum.magicball.net/showthread.php?t=14975"]here[/URL]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Please make sure that you also read the game FAQ before posting <a href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=22&amp;Itemid=21">here</a></p>\r

<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">We got a new domain name for  our website,you can now find us at <a href="http://www.lbanet.net/" target="_blank">www.lbanet.net</a></span></p>\r
<p><br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"> Furthemore we got a new small  release today featuring a new inventory item and a new feature.</span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p /><span style="font-size: 12pt;" /> \r
","</span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r

19,"test comment","test-comment","",":lol: :-$ :-# testage","",-2,3,0,3,"2010-07-04 10:55:58",66,"Rincevent","2010-07-04 10:58:45",66,0,"0000-00-00 00:00:00","0000-00-00 00:00:00","0000-00-00 00:00:00","","","",3,15,0,"","",0,2,""
20,"Introduction","introduction","","<p><img style="margin-left: 5px; float: right;" alt="lbanet_screen2" src="images/stories/lbanet_screen2.png" height="325" width="400" /></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">LBANet is a multiplayer game based on the original game Little Big Adventure. </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">The game is written in C++ and is open source for the client and also the server part. You can find the source code [URL=http://code.google.com/p/lbanet/]here[/URL]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">The game was designed to be multiplatform but we are currently only supporting Windows platforms because of a lack of time. However as the source is open and only use multiplatform library so if you are interested in porting the game over other platform just contact the team and we can help you there.</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">The game uses OpenGL as rendering engine. Thanks to that we do not use an isometric view anymore but a real 3D perspective view. You can have a look by yourself on the attached picture.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">[B]Current  game features:[/B]</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">[LIST] [*]walk twinsen through all original lba1 maps but also a few lba2 maps [*]play ingame music for each maps mp3 format) [*]you can change stances like in the original game,in addition to that you can also ride horse and dinofly through exterior maps. [*]twinsen has a life bar and will loose life if you fall down from to high or if you touch spikes. He will die if he has no more life. He will also drown if you go over water [*]in game chat with multiple channels but also with browser based application[*]support of smileys and color in the game chat [*]you can connect the game to the MBN IRC channel [*]support for in game videos in avi format [*]support for mikshape 3d model importing [*]the game is totally modular. You can create your own maps or even your own world and share it to the community. [*]inventory feature [*] You can talk to NPC and get quests from there [*]support for game fight system including magic ball and other projectiles not yet fully implemented)[/LIST]</p>","",1,2,0,5,"2010-07-05 15:10:46",62,"","2010-08-31 15:55:19",66,0,"0000-00-00 00:00:00","2010-07-05 15:10:46","0000-00-00 00:00:00","","","show_title=

21,"Getting started","getting-started","","<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">First you will need to install the game on your computer. To so so follow the instructions given in <a target="_blank" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9&amp;Itemid=11">here</a>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Some software is required prior to run Lbanet. So make sure that you have them installed on your machine before installing Lbanet as it is explained in the instructions.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Once you have installed the game on your machine,you can proceed to starting the game.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">If you downloaded the archive version,unpack it somewhere on your machine and start the LBANet.exe to patch the game.<br /> In case of installer version,run both installers then start Lbanet from the windows start menu. This will automatically run the game patcher.</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p>A screen should appear showing the game patcher:</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <img style="vertical-align: middle;" alt="patcher" src="images/stories/patcher.png" height="201" width="254" /></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">The game patcher is used to get the latest version of Lbanet from the server. It is automatically patching the game. All you need to do is wait for patching completion. You can then click the "Play" button on the screen to start the game.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">The game should then start showing you the login page:</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <img style="vertical-align: middle;" alt="login" src="images/stories/login.png" height="202" width="260" /></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Just enter your username and password and press the login button. if you  do not have an username yet you can get one by registering <strong><a target="_blank" href="index.php?option=com_comprofiler&amp;task=registers&amp;Itemid=12">here</a></strong>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Once logged in just select a world and press Enter or Ok button. You will arrive to the game view. Now the fun can start! for more details on the game gameplay you can have a look at the gameplay videos <strong><a href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=24&amp;Itemid=23">here</a></strong>)</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Troubleshooting:</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">If the game patcher or the game do not start or crash at startup first have a look at the FAQ section to see if your problem is known <strong><a target="_blank" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=22&amp;Itemid=21">here</a></strong></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">If you still can not resolve your problem,you can leave a post on the forum <strong><a target="_blank" href="http://forum.magicball.net/showthread.php?t=14975">here</a></strong>. You should get an answer from the community to help you out.</p>","",1,2,0,5,"2010-07-05 15:11:11",62,"","2010-08-31 15:47:38",62,0,"0000-00-00 00:00:00","2010-07-05 15:11:11","0000-00-00 00:00:00","","","show_title=

22,"FAQ","faq","","<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Do I need to pay something to play the game?<br /> </b>The game is free to play. However you should keep in mind that this game is a modification of the original game Little Big Adventure. So you need to own a copy of the  original LBA1 and LBA2 games in order to be allowed to play this game.<br /> <b><br /> <br /> The game just crashes after installation,it does not even start:<br /> </b>First make sure that you have the .NET platform 3.5 installed on  your machine,you can find it <a target="_blank" href="http://www.microsoft.com/downloads/details.aspx?FamilyId=333325FD-AE52-4E35-B531-508D977D32A6&amp;displaylang=en">here</a>.<br /> Also make sure that the visual C++ 2008 redistribuable is also  installed,you can find it <a target="_blank" href="http://www.microsoft.com/downloads/details.aspx?FamilyID=9b2da534-3e03-4391-8a4d-074b9f2bc1bf&amp;displaylang=en">here</a>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">In order to play the  game you will also need to install nvidia PhysX on your machine if you  do no have it already,you can download it <a target="_blank" href="http://www.nvidia.com/object/physx-9.10.0223-driver.html">here</a></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Finally make sure you have correctly followed the <a target="_self" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9:game-installation&amp;catid=5&amp;Itemid=11">installation instructions</a> and  check wether your operating system is supported,for example the game will not run over windows 2000.<br /> <br /> <b> <br /> I can not connect to the game server,an error message tells me "Server  version mismatch - please update your game"</b>:<br /> You do not have the latest version of the client,please update your  game using the game patcher.<br /> <br /> <br /> <br /> <b>I can start the game and run it but the game is really slow:</b><br /> It often come from the fact that your video card driver does not support  OpenGL correctly. <br /> Please make sure that you install the latest driver from your card  manufacturer and not from windows.<br /> <br /> <br /> <br /> <b>When I connect to a map I can see twinsen but the rest is blank or  look like this: </b><br /> <img alt="eek1" src="images/stories/eek1.jpg" height="113" width="153" /><br /> You did not install the bricks images files,please check the <a target="_self" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9:game-installation&amp;catid=5&amp;Itemid=11"> installation instruction</a> there to see how to do it.<br /> <br /> <br /> <b>The game patcher does not seem to work properly,I can not get  updates:<br /> </b>First check the patching.log file created in the lbanet.exe to see  if you get an error message there. Then make sure that your firewall  does not block LBANet.exe. If so please add LBANet.exe but also  patchingclient.exe to your firewall allowed list.<br /> <br /> <br /> <b>The map looks horrible,there is a lot of glitches or holes in there!</b><br /> This is due to the fact that we build a real 3D view out of 2D sprites.  So we get a perspective view but then we also get a lot of glitches. <br /> This is a trade off so if you really do not like how the game looks,you  can reset the view to isometric under the game option.<br /> <br /> <br /> <b>I found a bug! What shall I do? Is this game of so poor  quality?</b><br /> Keep in mind that the game is made by a very small team. Do not expect  to get a professionnal game from today to tomorrow. <br /> We are constantly in the proccess to update and clean game content. So  if you find a bug please post it here:<a href="http://sacredcarrot.xesf.net/mantis/main_page.php" target="_blank"> </a><a href="http://sacredcarrot.xesf.net/mantis/main_page.php" target="_blank">http://sacredcarrot.xesf.net/mantis/main_page.php</a>. We will then try  to solve it asap.<br /> <br /> <br /> <strong>I like the game and I would like to help,what can I do?</strong><br /> All the help is accepted as long as you are motivated. Here is a list of  some possible tasks to be done:</p>\r
<ul>\r
<li>Game testing try to find glitches in the game and  report them in the bugtracker).</li>\r
<li>Creating a short video trailer of the game.</li>\r
<li>Creating some new worlds for the game,now all the tools are  available so just try them out!</li>\r
<li>Porting and maintaining LBANet over Linux</li>\r
<li>Porting and maintaining LBANet over Mac OSX</li>\r
<li>If you are a C++ programmer,we are looking for someone to port the  game under OpenSG engine</li>\r
<li>Create stories and dialogs for LBANet</li>\r
</ul>\r
<p>In any case,just send me a PM user Rincevent then we can discuss together about  how you would help the best.</p>","",1,2,0,5,"2010-07-05 15:11:37",62,"","2010-08-31 15:54:40",62,0,"0000-00-00 00:00:00","2010-07-05 15:11:37","0000-00-00 00:00:00","","","show_title=

27,"New Release v0.91 - new website","new-release-v091-new-website","","<p><img style="margin-left: 10px; float: right;" alt="mailbox" src="images/stories/mailbox.png" height="150" width="150" /></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">Lbanet has a new website featuring a lot of new stuff.</span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;"><br /></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">Now the Lbanet community will be able to keep in touch via the website</span><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">.                                 <br /></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;"><br /></span></p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">In addition to that website and game are now in sync...</span></p>\r
<p /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;" /> \r
","\r
</span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">Here is the complete list of new features:</span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><br /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">- the website now support mulitple languages not yet fully translated)</span></p>\r

39,"New game engine demo","new-game-engine-demo","","<p style="text-align: justify;"><img style="float: right;" alt="lba2map150" src="images/stories/lba2map150.png" height="150" width="150" /></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">As promised here is a demo if the new game engine,featuring LBA2 outside maps a well as full 3D camera. You can download the demo <a href="http://neolbanet.googlecode.com/files/lbanet_1.0_demo.rar">here</a>.</span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;">This new engine will come with a lot of additionnal features to make the game more enjoyable.<br /></span></p>\r
<p /><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt; color: #a7fafa;" /> \r
","\r
</span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">The new engine is still under development and this is only a demo version only working in local mode not the full game. Once completed,it will have the following features in addition to the existing one):</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- complete fighting system  projectile and body contact e.g. saber)</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;"><br /></span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- new display engine using <a href="http://www.openscenegraph.org">OSG </a>with the following extensions:</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- full 3D environment,being able to display any type of map LBA1 grids,LBA2 outside maps,custom maps)<br /></span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- real-time lighting system including shadows</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- integration with shaders</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- can include models animated or not) from any known design tools blender,3dsmax,...)</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- particle system</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- fog<br /></span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify; padding-left: 30px;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;"><br /></span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- integration with LUA for extended scripting NPCs behaviors,custom triggers in game,...)</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- 1 server per world giving the world creator more freedom. He will be able to update his world and restart his server at any time whithout interfering with the other worlds.</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">The demo includes 3 worlds in order to show the new engine potential:</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;"> - The original lba1 prison map</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- A world containing all Lba2 external islands</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- A world containing a map made with custom bricks made by mazaka</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">The controls are the same than lbanet,with some additions:</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- F10 takes a screenshot</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- F11 show the FPS and other stats</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- F12 toggle the fullscreen</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">- Right shift center the camera on twinsen same as enter key in original LBA2 game)</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">In the option video tab you have a new combobox giving you the choice of camera type. You can play with it and see the different possibilities. Leaving it to auto will let the game decide which camera is the best depedning of the type of map.</span></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #a7fafa;"><span style="font-family: tahoma,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">Hope you enjoy the demo. Any comments are welcome :)<br /></span></span></p>",1,2,0,1,"2010-10-10 17:41:36",66,"","2010-10-24 19:19:24",66,0,"0000-00-00 00:00:00","2010-10-10 17:39:12","0000-00-00 00:00:00","","","show_title=

225,3,9,"content","introtext","<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><b>Avant d’installer le jeu,assurez-vous que vous avez la plate-forme .NET 3.5 installée sur votre ordinateur. Si non,vous pouvez le télécharger&nbsp; </b><strong>&nbsp;</strong><a target="_blank" href="http://www.microsoft.com/downloads/details.aspx?FamilyId=333325FD-AE52-4E35-B531-508D977D32A6&amp;displaylang=en">ici</a></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><b>Afin de jouer au jeu,vous avez aussi besoin d’installer nvidia PhysX sur votre ordinateur si vous ne l’avez pas déjà. Vous pouvez le télécharger </b><a target="_blank" href="http://www.nvidia.com/object/physx-9.10.0223-driver.html">ici.</a></span></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p>Il y a deux manières d""installer le jeu sur votre ordinateur :</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><b>En utilisant les installateurs recommandé pour windows XP) : </b></p>\r
<p style="padding-left: 30px;">1. Télécharger et installer l""installateur du jeu : <a href="http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LbanetSetup.msi" target="_blank">http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LbanetSetup.msi</a></p>\r
<p style="padding-left: 30px;">2. Télécharger et installer l""installateur des fichiers images : <a href="http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LbanetImageSetup.msi" target="_blank">http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LbanetImageSetup.msi</a></p>\r
<p style="padding-left: 30px;">3. Démarrer le jeu depuis le menu Démarrer ou par un raccourci bureau</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><b>Installation manuelle depuis les fichiers archives recommandé pour windows vista et 7) :</b></p>\r
<p style="padding-left: 30px;">1. Télécharger et décompresser l""archive du jeu : <a href="http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LBANet_v0.7.rar">http://lbanet.googlecode.com/files/LBANet_v0.7.rar</a></p>\r
<p style="padding-left: 30px;">2. Lancer LBANet.exe</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><b>Configuration du jeu :</b></p>\r
<p style="padding-left: 30px;">1. Le jeu a été testé sous: Windows XP,Windows Vista 32bit et 64bit) et Windows  7 32bit et 64bit). <br /> 2. Il a été également testé et peut fonctionner sous Mac OSX avec Parallels<br /> 3. Il n""existe pas de version prise en charge pour Linux actuellement,mais c""est prévu<br /> 4. Le jeu ne tourne pas sous Windows 2000 car le protocole IPV6 n""y est pas pris en charge.<br /> 5. Il n""y a pas de réelles configurations minimales requises,toutefois  votre carte graphique à besoin d""avoir des pilotes supportant l""OpenGL  pour le jeu afin de fonctionner correctement. Votre carte graphique a  également besoin de supporter une taille de texture d""au moins 2048X2048</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="color: #ff0000;"><b>Utilisateurs de windows 7 et vista&nbsp;: le jeu et le patcheur du jeu  ont besoin d’être exécuté en tant qu’administrateur. Pour ce faire, allez dans le répertoire du jeu. Faites un clic droit sur Lbanet.exe.  Cliquez sur Propriétés dans le menu qui s’est ouvert. Allez à l’onglet  Compatibilité. Cochez la case «&nbsp;Exécuter en tant qu’administrateur&nbsp;».  Cliquez sur le bouton OK.</b></span></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p><span style="color: #ff0000;"><b><br /></b></span></p>\r

307,3,22,"content","introtext","<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Est-ce que j""ai besoin de payer quelque chose pour jouer au jeu ?</b></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Le jeu est gratuit. Toutefois vous devez garder à l’esprit que ce jeu est une modification du jeu original Little Big Adventure. Vous avez donc besoin de posséder une copie du jeu original LBA1 afin d’être autorisé à jouer ce jeu.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b><br /></b><b>Le jeu plante juste après l""installation,il ne veut pas se lancer:<br /> </b>Premièrement,assurez-vous d""avoir la plate-forme.NET 3.5&nbsp;installée sur votre ordinateur,à télécharger <a target="_blank" href="http://www.microsoft.com/downloads/details.aspx?FamilyId=333325FD-AE52-4E35-B531-508D977D32A6&amp;displaylang=en">ici</a>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Assurez-vous également que le Visual C++ 2008 Redistributable est également installé,à télécharger  <a target="_blank" href="http://www.microsoft.com/downloads/details.aspx?FamilyID=9b2da534-3e03-4391-8a4d-074b9f2bc1bf&amp;displaylang=en">ici</a>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Afin de jouer au jeu vous avez aussi besoin d’installer nvidia PhysX sur votre ordinateur si vous ne l’avez pas déjà. Vous pouvez le télécharger&nbsp;<a target="_blank" href="http://www.nvidia.com/object/physx-9.10.0223-driver.html">ici</a></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Enfin,assurez-vous que vous avez correctement suivi les <a target="_self" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9:game-installation&amp;catid=5&amp;Itemid=11">instructions d""installation</a> et vérifiez si votre système d""exploitation peut le supporter,par exemple,le jeu ne fonctionnera pas sous Windows 2000.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><br /> <b> <br /></b></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Je n""arrive à me connecter au serveur du jeu,un message d""erreur me dit «&nbsp; Server version mismatch - please update your game&nbsp;La version du serveur ne correspond pas – veuillez mettre votre jeu à jour)&nbsp;» :</b><br /> Vous n""avez pas la dernière version du serveur,mettez votre jeu à jour grâce au patcheur du jeu.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Je peux lancez le jeu et y jouer mais il est vraiment lent:</b><br /> Cela provient souvent du fait que le pilote de votre carte graphique ne prend pas en charge l""OpenGL correctement. Veuillez vous assurer d""avoir installé le dernier pilote depuis le fabricant de votre carte graphique et non depuis Windows.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Quand je me connecte à une carte,je peux voir Twinsen mais le reste est blanc ou ressemble à ceci:</b></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><img alt="eek1" src="images/stories/eek1.jpg" height="113" width="153" /></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Vous n""avez pas installé les fichiers images,veuillez vérifier les <a target="_self" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9:game-installation&amp;catid=5&amp;Itemid=11">i</a><a target="_self" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9:game-installation&amp;catid=5&amp;Itemid=11">instructions d""installation</a> pour savoir comment procéder.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><br /> <br /></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Le patcheur du jeu ne semble pas fonctionner correctement,je ne peux pas avoir de mises à jour:</b><br /> Premièrement,vérifiez le fichier patching.log créé dans lbanet.exe pour voir si vous recevez un message d""erreur. Assurez-vous ensuite que votre pare-feu ne bloque pas Lbanet.exe. Si c""est le cas,ajoutez Lbanet.exe ainsi que patchingclient.exe à la liste des programmes autorisés par votre pare-feu.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>La carte est horrible à voir,il y a énormément de défauts ou de trous!</b><br /> Cela est dû au fait que nous construisons une vue 3D réelle à partir d""icônes 2D. Nous obtenons ainsi une vue en perspective mais nous obtenons également beaucoup de défauts. Il s""agit d""un compromis,si vous n""aimez donc vraiment pas le jeu tel qu""il est présenté,vous pouvez rétablir la vue isométrique dans les options du jeu.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><b>J""ai trouvé un bug! Que dois-je faire? Est-ce que ce jeu est de si mauvaise qualité?</b></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Gardez à l""esprit que le jeu est conçu par une très petite équipe. Ne vous attendez pas à obtenir un jeu professionnel du jour au lendemain. Nous sommes constamment occupés à mettre le jeu à jour et à nettoyer son contenu. Si vous trouvez donc un bug,postez-le ici:<a href="http://sacredcarrot.xesf.net/mantis/main_page.php" target="_blank"> http://sacredcarrot.xesf.net/mantis/main_page.php</a>. Nous essaierons ensuite de le résoudre dès que possible.</p>\r

<p style="text-align: justify;">Premièrement,vous avez besoin d’installer le jeu sur votre ordinateur. Pour ce faire,suivez les instructions données <a target="_blank" href="index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=9&amp;Itemid=11">ici</a>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Certains logiciels sont nécessaires avant de lancer Lbanet. Assurez-vous donc que vous les avez installés sur votre ordinateur avant d’installer Lbanet comme c’est expliqué dans les instructions.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Une fois le jeu installé sur votre ordinateur,vous pouvez maintenant commencer à jouer.<br /> Pour ce faire,si vous avez installé le jeu en utilisant l’installateur,une nouvelle icône devrait apparaitre dans le menu de démarrage. Cliquez simplement sur cette icône. Pour ceux qui ont installé le jeu depuis l’archive. Lancez LBANet.exe depuis le dossier du jeu.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r

<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <img style="vertical-align: middle;" alt="patcher" src="images/stories/patcher.png" height="201" width="254" /></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Le patcheur du jeu est utilisé pour avoir la dernière version de Lbanet depuis le serveur. Le jeu est automatiquement mis à jour. Tout ce que vous avez à faire,c’est d’attendre la fin de la mise à jour. Vous pouvez ensuite cliquer sur le bouton «&nbsp;Jouer&nbsp;» à l’écran.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Le jeu devrait alors être lancé affichant la page de connexion&nbsp;:</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <img style="vertical-align: middle;" alt="login" src="images/stories/login.png" height="202" width="260" /></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Entrez simplement votre nom d’utilisateur et votre mot de passe et appuyez sur le bouton de connexion. Si vous n’avez pas encore de nom d’utilisateur,vous pouvez en avoir un en vous inscrivant <strong><a target="_blank" href="index.php?option=com_comprofiler&amp;task=registers&amp;Itemid=12">ici</a></strong>.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r

361,3,20,"content","introtext","<p><img style="margin-left: 5px; float: right;" alt="lbanet_screen2" src="images/stories/lbanet_screen2.png" height="325" width="400" /></p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Lbanet est un jeu multijoueur basé sur le jeu original Little Big Adventure.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Le jeu est écrit en C++ et le code source est&nbsp; libre pour le jeu ainsi que pour la partie serveur. Vous pouvez trouver le code source <a target="_blank" href="http://code.google.com/p/lbanet/">ici.</a></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Le jeu a été conçu pour être multiplateforme mais nous ne supportons actuellement que les plates-formes Windows à cause d’un manque de ressources. Cependant,le code source est libre et le moteur de jeu n’utilise que des composants multiplateformes. Donc si vous êtes intéressés afin de transposer le jeu sur une des autres plate-formes,contactez simplement l’équipe et nous pourrons alors vous aider.</p>\r
<p> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;">Le jeu utilise OpenGL comme moteur de rendu. Grâce à cela,le jeu n’est pas en vue isométrique comme pour l’original mais il utilise une vue en perspective 3D réelle. Vous pouvez voir par vous-même sur l’image ci-dessus.</p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Caractéristiques actuelles du moteur de jeu:</strong></p>\r
<p style="text-align: justify;"> </p>\r
<ol>\r
<li>Twinsen voyage à travers toutes les cartes originales de lba1 mais aussi quelques cartes de lba2</li>\r
<li>Musique du jeu jouée pour chaque carte</li>\r
<li>Vous pouvez changer de comportement comme dans le jeu original,en plus de cela vous&nbsp; pouvez aussi monter à cheval et en dino-fly en extérieur.</li>\r
<li>Twinsen a une barre de vie et perdra de la vie si vous tombez de haut ou si vous touchez des piques. Il mourra s’il n’a plus de vie.&nbsp; Il se noiera également si vous allez dans l’eau.</li>\r
<li>Vous pouvez discuter en jeu grâce à différents canaux de discussion</li>\r
<li>Utilisation d’émoticônes et de couleur dans la fenêtre de discussion du jeu</li>\r
<li>Vous pouvez connecter le jeu au canal IRC du MBN.</li>\r
<li>Supporte le format avi pour les vidéos du jeu</li>\r
<li>Supporte l’importation des modèles 3d « MIKSHAPE »</li>\r
<li>Le jeu est totalement modulable. Vous pouvez créer vos propres cartes voire même votre propre monde et le partager à la communauté.</li>\r
<li>Système d’inventaire</li>\r
<li>Vous pouvez parler aux PNJ et recevoir des quêtes</li>\r
<li>Système de combat en jeu incluant la balle magique et d’autres projectiles pas encore complètement implémenté)</li>\r
</ol>","7822722fde2a99f546bf778529a7693d","","2010-08-04 15:05:56",62,1

Je vois que la dernier new n\\""a pas été traduite,et je ne vois pas de fanlba à l\\""horizon,donc je me suis lancé...\r
\r
J\\""ai eu du mal à traduire \\"crash report\\",si tu as une meilleure traduction,n\\""hésite pas à remplacer celle-ci... ^^\\""\r
J\\""ai eu un peu de mal avec \\"movable objects\\" aussi... J\\""aurais pu mettre \\"objets déplaçable\\" partout,mais ça aurait fait trop de répétitions...\r
Le temple de Bu,en français,ça prend un accent?\r
\r
J\\""espère que ma traduction est pas trop mal et que tu n\\""y verra pas trop de trucs à changer... ^^\\""\r
\r
\r
\r
L\\""équipe est heureuse de vous annoncer un nouvelle mise à jour incluant les objets mouvant.\r
\r
De plus,l\\""animation des personnages et leur vitesse de déplacement son désormais en parfaite synchronisation...\r
\r
Voici la liste complète des ajouts:\r
\r
- Certains objets peuvent maintenant être déplacés caisses,statues)\r
\r
- Une nouvelle quête a été ajoutée dans le port de l\\""île de la Citadelle parlez au Grobo près de l\\""entrepôt pour y accéder)\r
\r
- Les objets à déplacer peuvent prendre les monte-charges ou activer les interrupteurs au sol. Vous pouvez essayer ceci au temple de Bu,en utilisant la statue pour activer l\\""interrupteur de la porte.\r
\r
- Les objets mouvant sont dupliqués sur l\\""ordinateur des autres joueurs sous forme d\\""image fantôme.\r
\r
- L\\""animation des personnages et leur vitesse de déplacement sont maintenant synchronisés. Essayez les comportements \\"discret\\" ou \\"agressif\\" pour voir la différence. Vous pouvez également le remarquer lorsque vous grimpez une échelle.\r
\r
- Un \\"crash reporter\\" a été ajouté au jeu. Dans le cas où votre jeu plante,une fenêtre apparaîtra pour vous demander d\\""envoyer un rapport de bug au forum du Magic Ball Network. Si vous souhaitez que le jeu s\\""améliore et devienne plus stable,merci de poster les rapport de vos bugs,cela nous aidera sûrement beaucoup!\r
\r
J\\""espère que vous aimerez cette mise à jour.  Nous allons maintenant fermer le sondage et commencer à travailler sur le prochain ajout: le combat avec les monstres. Merci de donner votre avis. Il y aura d\\""autres sondages comme celui-ci à l\\""avenir,donc restez connectés! ;)
